**<span style="font-size:14.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Python Unit Testing Objectives</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895901696;margin-left:0px;margin-top:9px;width:967px;height:1px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image001.jpg" width="967" height="1" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use the built-in unittest package to write unit tests</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

[<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#4078C0;text-decoration:
none">unittest</span>](https://docs.python.org/3.8/library/unittest.html)

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895900672"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Built in to python</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895899648"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Requires that you build a class that inherits from </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">unittest.TestCase</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895898624"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-7px;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">test functions must start with </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">test\_</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895896576"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895895552"><span style="position:absolute;

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;

<span style="position:relative;

width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="position:relative;

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;

z-index:-1895873024"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;

font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Creates a virtual installation of python. Uses symbolic links and adjustments</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895872000"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">to certain environment variables to isolate python packages from one project</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">to another.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Can be used standalone but we used it mostly by leveraging pipenv which uses</span>

<span style="position:relative;

width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Demonstrate how to use pipenv to initialize a project and install dependencies</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

[<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#4078C0;text-decoration:none">pipenv</span>](https://pipenv.pypa.io/en/latest/)

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895868928"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Combines </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pip</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> and </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">virtualenv</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> into one command.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895867904"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895866880"><span style="position:absolute;
left:97px;top:-12px;width:112px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image014.jpg" width="112" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Creates a virtual environment using </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">virtualenv</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895865856"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895864832"><span style="position:absolute;
left:220px;top:-13px;width:64px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image015.jpg" width="64" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Uses </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pip</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> internally to install packages listed in a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Pipfile</span><span style="font-size:
8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> .</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895863808"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895862784"><span style="position:absolute;
left:72px;top:-12px;width:24px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image016.jpg" width="24" height="14" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895861760"><span style="position:absolute;
left:290px;top:-12px;width:46px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image017.jpg" width="46" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Locks packages to specific versions with a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Pipfile.lock</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> .</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895860736"><span style="position:absolute;left:31px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image003.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895859712"><span style="position:absolute;
left:254px;top:-12px;width:74px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image018.jpg" width="74" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Uses an environment variable named </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">PIPENV\_VENV\_IN\_PROJECT</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> . When set to </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">1</span>

<span style="position:relative;

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Describe how modules and packages are found and loaded from import statements</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">First some definitions:</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Module </span>*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">: a single .py file or a directory with a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_init\_\_.py</span>*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> </span>*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">file can be</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895840256"><span style="position:absolute;left:220px;top:-13px;
width:69px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image027.jpg" width="69" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">considered a module</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Package </span>*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">: a collection of modules and submodules in a directory</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Submodule </span>*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">: a python module inside a sub directory of a module</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Python Path</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">The Python Path is a list of directories python looks for modules in.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:141%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">When you import a module, python searches these directories for a file module or directory module (with a **init**.py file in it) that matches the name you are trying to import.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can inspect the python path from python by printing </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sys.path</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895839232"><span style="position:absolute;left:274px;top:-12px;
width:52px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image028.jpg" width="52" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can add directories to the python path by setting the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">PYTHON\_PATH</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895838208"><span style="position:absolute;left:277px;top:-13px;
width:69px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image027.jpg" width="69" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">environment variable.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Luckily we have tools like </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">virtualenv</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> and </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> which means we do not have</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895837184"><span style="position:absolute;left:127px;top:-13px;
width:129px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image029.jpg" width="129" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">to worry as much about setting the Python path manually.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Exporting</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Inside a python script, any variables, functions or classes are automatically</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">exported and can be imported by name.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">If you want to control which things get exported from a python module you can</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
line-height:80%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">set the variable </span><span style="font-size:.5pt;line-height:80%"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image030.jpg" id="Picture 162" data-border="0" width="46" height="10" /></span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:80%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> equal to a list of strings representing the things</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">to export.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">The Rules</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Using the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">import</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> statement</span>**

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895836160"><span style="position:absolute;left:53px;top:-12px;
width:41px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image005.jpg" width="41" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">When you import a .py file as a module, it searches </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">sys.path</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> for a file with</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895835136"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895834112"><span style="position:absolute;
left:275px;top:-13px;width:52px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image028.jpg" width="52" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">that name and runs that file.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">When you import a directory as a module, it also searches </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">sys.path</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> for a</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895833088"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895832064"><span style="position:absolute;
left:308px;top:-13px;width:52px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image028.jpg" width="52" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:80%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">directory with that name and runs the </span><span style="font-size:.5pt;line-height:80%"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image031.jpg" id="Picture 168" data-border="0" width="69" height="10" /></span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:80%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> contained in that directory.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Using the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">python</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> command line interpreter</span>**

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895831040"><span style="position:absolute;left:53px;top:-12px;
width:41px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image005.jpg" width="41" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">When you run a .py file it runs that file</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895830016"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:absolute;z-index:-1895828992;margin-left:9px;margin-top:11px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:80%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">When you run a directory it runs </span><span style="font-size:
.5pt;line-height:80%"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image031.jpg" id="Picture 172" data-border="0" width="69" height="10" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">When you run a directory with the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">-m</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> option, it searches </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">sys.path</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> for the module and runs both the </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_init\_\_.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> and the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_main\_\_.py</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895827968"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895826944"><span style="position:absolute;
left:189px;top:-12px;width:19px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image032.jpg" width="19" height="14" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895825920"><span style="position:absolute;
left:303px;top:-12px;width:52px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image028.jpg" width="52" height="14" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895824896"><span style="position:absolute;
left:520px;top:-12px;width:181px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image033.jpg" width="181" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Most of the time we'll use </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_init\_\_.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> not </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_main\_\_.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> when we build our own</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895823872"><span style="position:absolute;left:126px;top:-13px;
width:160px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image034.jpg" width="160" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">modules.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Documentation on import</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

[<span style="font-size:
8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#4078C0;text-decoration:none">Import System</span>](https://docs.python.org/3/reference/import.html)

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895822848"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

[<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#4078C0;text-decoration:
none">Import Statement</span>](https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#import)

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895821824"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Describe the purpose of and when init.py runs</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">When you run a directory with the </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">-m</span><span style="font-size:
8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> option, or when you import a directory,</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895820800"><span style="position:absolute;left:167px;top:-13px;
width:19px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image035.jpg" width="19" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">\_\_init\_\_.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> file executes. The purpose of </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_init\_\_.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> to be able to</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895819776"><span style="position:absolute;left:18px;top:-12px;
width:69px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image036.jpg" width="69" height="15" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895818752"><span style="position:absolute;
left:235px;top:-12px;width:69px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image036.jpg" width="69" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">build python packages and subdivide the packages into multiple sub-modules.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Describe the purpose of and when main.py runs</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">When you run a directory as a regular python program (not with </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">-m</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> ) the</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895817728"><span style="position:absolute;left:312px;top:-12px;
width:18px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image037.jpg" width="18" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_main\_\_.py </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">file is executed. The purpose of</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333"> \_\_main\_\_.py </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">is to allow us</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895816704"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-12px;
width:69px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image027.jpg" width="69" height="14" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895815680"><span style="position:absolute;
left:228px;top:-12px;width:69px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image027.jpg" width="69" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">to execute a directory as if it was a python program.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:14.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Flask Objectives</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895814656;margin-left:0px;margin-top:9px;width:967px;height:1px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image001.jpg" width="967" height="1" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Setup a new Flask project</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Flask is a python based web application server. It is a backend framework</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">similar to Express.js</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">First, you should install Flask into a virtual environment</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895813632;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv install flask</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Create a python script to start your application. This might be </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> or</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895812608"><span style="position:absolute;left:300px;top:-12px;
width:41px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image038.jpg" width="41" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">another script which imports an </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app/\_\_init.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> module.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895811584"><span style="position:absolute;left:155px;top:-13px;
width:81px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image039.jpg" width="81" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">This is the bare minimum needed to make Flask application:</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<table data-cellspacing="0" data-cellpadding="0" data-hspace="0" data-vspace="0" width="79" height="8"><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;" data-valign="top" height="8" style="padding-top: 0in; padding-right: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0in"><p><span id="page4"></span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:79%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from_object()</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<table data-cellspacing="0" data-cellpadding="0" data-hspace="0" data-vspace="0" width="79" height="8"><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;" data-valign="top" height="8" style="padding-top: 0in; padding-right: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0in"><p><span style="font-size:6.5pt;
  line-height:79%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">python-dotenv</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895810560;margin-left:45px;margin-top:37px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask **import** Flask</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app = Flask(\_\_name\_\_)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Flask requires that you set an environment variable called </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">FLASK\_APP</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> before</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895809536"><span style="position:absolute;left:284px;top:-13px;
width:58px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image041.jpg" width="58" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">it will run. It needs to be set to the name of your flask application script</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">or module. You could put this into a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.env</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> file and let </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> load it</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895808512"><span style="position:absolute;left:174px;top:-13px;
width:128px;height:32px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image042.jpg" width="128" height="32" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
line-height:77%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">or use the </span><span style="font-size:.5pt;line-height:77%"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image043.jpg" id="Picture 193" data-border="0" width="80" height="10" /></span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:77%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> module to load a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:77%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.flaskenv</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:77%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> file.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Often you might use the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.flaskenv</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> file to load environment variables like</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895807488"><span style="position:absolute;left:120px;top:-12px;
width:58px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image041.jpg" width="58" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">FLASK\_APP </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">and checking it into source control, and reserve the</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> .env </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">file for</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895806464"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-12px;
width:58px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image041.jpg" width="58" height="15" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895805440"><span style="position:absolute;
left:313px;top:-12px;width:30px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image025.jpg" width="30" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">secret information like passwords or database configurations.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Run a simple Flask web application on your computer</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Once you have your application setup, you can just run it with flask.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895804416;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run flask run</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Utilize basic configuration on a Flask project</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can use the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.config</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> dictionary to hold Flask configuration values.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895803392"><span style="position:absolute;left:82px;top:-12px;
width:63px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image044.jpg" width="63" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">An even better way to setup your flask app is to create a python module with a</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">configuration class in it. This class just needs properties for each</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">configuration variable. Then you can import the class, and use the</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">method to load it into the app's config dictionary.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895802368;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:84px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image045.jpg" width="967" height="84" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># config.py</span>*

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">Config</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">SOME\_CONFIG\_VARIABLE = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Some value'</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895801344;margin-left:0px;margin-top:35px;width:967px;height:136px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image046.jpg" width="967" height="136" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">app.py</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Import the config class </span>***<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">config **import** Config</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app = Flask(\_\_name\_\_)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Load the config into Flask. </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.config.from\_object(Config)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can access any config variables in your flask app by just referencing</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">them on the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.config</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> dictionary.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895800320;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895799296"><span style="position:absolute;
left:61px;top:-13px;width:64px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image047.jpg" width="64" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.config\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'SOME\_CONFIG\_VARIABLE'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Create a static route in Flask</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">A static route is one that just routes to a path without any parameters.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895798272;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:162px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image048.jpg" width="967" height="162" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Examples</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.route('/') </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">index</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"""Put code here to execute when \`/\` is visited""" </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pass</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.route('/somepath')</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">some\_path</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"""Put code here to execute when \`/somepath\` is visited"""</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pass</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Create a parameterized route in Flask</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">A parameterized route uses </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">&lt;&gt;</span><span style="font-size:
8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> characters to declare that part of a path</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895797248"><span style="position:absolute;left:138px;top:-13px;
width:19px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image035.jpg" width="19" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">should be a parameter.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895796224;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">the &lt;id> parameter will be captured and passed into the function as the first</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">argument</span>*

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.route('/item/&lt;id>')</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">item</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(id):</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">f'&lt;h1>Item</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{id}</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">&lt;/h1>'</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895795200;margin-left:0px;margin-top:35px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">You can also specify the type of the parameter by prepending it with the type</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">and a colon</span>*

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.route('/item/&lt;int:id>')</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">item</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(id):</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">f'&lt;h1>Item</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{id}</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">&lt;/h1>'</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use decorators run code before and after requests</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">The </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">@app.before\_request</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> and </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">@app.after\_request</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> happen before and after</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895794176"><span style="position:absolute;left:22px;top:-13px;
width:247px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image050.jpg" width="247" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">every request to the server. Use them to do any initialization or cleanup</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">you need to happen on each request</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895793152;margin-left:-1px;margin-top:17px;width:969px;height:43px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image051.jpg" width="969" height="43" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.before\_request</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">before\_request\_function</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<table data-cellspacing="0" data-cellpadding="0" data-hspace="0" data-vspace="0" width="39" height="8"><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;" data-valign="top" height="8" style="padding-top: 0in; padding-right: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0in"><p><span id="page5"></span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:79%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class_</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"before\_request is running"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895792128"><span style="position:absolute;left:-1px;top:-10px;
width:969px;height:108px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image052.jpg" width="969" height="108" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.after\_request</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">after\_request\_function</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(response):</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"after\_request is running"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">response</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">@app.before\_first\_request </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">only happens once before the very first request</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895791104"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-12px;
width:148px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image053.jpg" width="148" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">to the server</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895790080;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.before\_first\_request</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">before\_first\_function</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"before\_first\_request happens once"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Identify the "static" route</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Don't confuse this with declaring a static route above. This is a special</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">built in route you don't have to define at all.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">If you create a folder called </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">static</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> then any requests to </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">/static</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> on your</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895789056"><span style="position:absolute;left:135px;top:-13px;
width:41px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image005.jpg" width="41" height="14" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895788032"><span style="position:absolute;
left:282px;top:-13px;width:47px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image055.jpg" width="47" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">server will cause flask to serve up the files contained in this folder.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895787008;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">http:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#009926">//</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">localhost:</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">5000</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#009926">/static/</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">styles</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#009926">/main.css</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895785984;margin-left:0px;margin-top:35px;width:967px;height:188px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image056.jpg" width="967" height="188" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">├── Pipfile</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">├── Pipfile.lock</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">├── app</span><span style="font-size:
10.0pt">                          </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">&lt;- **directory where** Flask **is** created</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">├── \_\_init\_\_.py  &lt;- **file in** which Flask **is** created</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">├── routes.py</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">├── **static**&lt;- **static** files served **from** here</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│   └── styles</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│</span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">└── main.css</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">└── templates</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">│<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">        </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">└── main.html</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">└── app\_loader.py</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use WTForms to define and render forms in Flask</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">WTForms is a python package that allows you to easily generate forms and form</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">fields. Flask-WTF is a companion python package that allows you to parse</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">POST data from a form and render the form fields.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You define your form as a class that inherits from the FlaskForm base class.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895784960;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask\_wtf **import** FlaskForm</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">SampleForm</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(FlaskForm):</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Then inside the class use WTForm fields on properties of the class.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895783936;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">SampleForm</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(FlaskForm):</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">name = StringField(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Name'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">In your route, you can instantiate an instance of your form and then pass</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">it to a view to be rendered.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895782912;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:123px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image057.jpg" width="967" height="123" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.sample\_form **import** SampleForm</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Create an instance of our form </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">form = SampleForm()</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">And pass it to the view template</span>*

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">render\_template(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'form.html'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, form=form)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Inside the view template, you can access the fields from the form to</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">output HTML for the form and it's fields.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895781888;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:136px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image046.jpg" width="967" height="136" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;form </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">action</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">""</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy"> </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">method</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"post"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy"> </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">novalidate</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&gt;</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{{ form.csrf\_token }} </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;p></span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{{ form.name.label }} {{ form.name(size=32) }}</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;/p></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;p></span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{{ form.submit() }}</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;/p></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;/form></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
