font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">The calls inside of the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{{ }}</span><span style="font-size:
8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> will output HTML.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895780864"><span style="position:absolute;left:109px;top:-13px;
width:36px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image058.jpg" width="36" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Because of some special python magic (the **call** and **str** methods on</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">FlaskForm), you can just use the properties without calling them, or call them with extra parameters, and both will work!</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Passing extra keyword parameters to the field instances will add HTML attributes</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">for those parameters. However, because </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> is a reserved word in Python,</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895779840"><span style="position:absolute;left:201px;top:-13px;
width:36px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image058.jpg" width="36" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:4.5pt;
line-height:75%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">you will have to use</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:75%">                              </span><span style="font-size:4.5pt;line-height:75%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">when you want to add a CSS class.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895778816;margin-left:0px;margin-top:30px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895777792"><span style="position:absolute;
left:99px;top:-1px;width:41px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image038.jpg" width="41" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">form.name(size=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">32</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, class\_=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'name'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page6"></span>**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Use WTForms to validate data in a POST with the built-in validators</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">To validate a form with Flask-WTF you can call the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">validate\_on\_submit</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> method</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895776768"><span style="position:absolute;left:249px;top:-13px;
width:108px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image059.jpg" width="108" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">on your form instance. This must be done inside of a route that handles </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">POST</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895775744"><span style="position:absolute;left:350px;top:-13px;
width:30px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image025.jpg" width="30" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">requests.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895774720;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:162px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image048.jpg" width="967" height="162" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.route('/submit', methods=\['POST'\])</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">handle\_form\_submit</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">if </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">form.validate\_on\_submit():</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Do something with the form data.</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">and return something</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">You can put code here to handle what happens when</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">the form fails validation, like redirecting or rendering</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">the form again.</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">It should be noted that </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">validate\_on\_submit</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> *automatically* reads the incoming</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895773696"><span style="position:absolute;left:112px;top:-12px;
width:108px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image059.jpg" width="108" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">parameters from the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">request</span><span style="font-size:
8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> object in Flask, so there's no reason to import it</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895772672"><span style="position:absolute;left:102px;top:-13px;
width:47px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image060.jpg" width="47" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">or use it manually.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">CSRF</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">To protect against Cross-Site Request Forgery attacks, Flask-Wtf automatically</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">generates and checks CSRF tokens. However we must add one of these two fields</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">in our form in order to print out the CSRF token.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895771648;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This one prints out ALL the hidden fields including the CSRF that are</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">defined on the form class</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{{ form.hidden\_tag() }</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">or</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895770624;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">While this one only prints out the CSRF token hidden field </span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{{ form.csrf\_token() }}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use the following basic field types in WTForms</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You use these by creating a class property on your class which inherits from</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">FlaskForm</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895769600;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">MyForm</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(FlaskForm):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">field1 = StringField()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">BooleanField</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">field.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

[<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#4078C0;text-decoration:
none">WTForms Field Documentation</span>](https://wtforms.readthedocs.io/en/2.3.x/fields/#module-wtforms.fields)

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Create a Flask Blueprint</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">A Flask Blueprint is a way to modularize our routes.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">In a new module, import Blueprint and create one like this:</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895753216;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:84px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image045.jpg" width="967" height="84" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># admin.py</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask **import** Blueprint</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">admin\_bp = Blueprint(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'admin'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, \_\_name\_\_, url\_prefix=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">'/admin'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Register the Flask Blueprint with the Flask application</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Then import it into your main Flask app file</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">and register it so Flask knows about the routes contained within.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895752192;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">admin **import** admin\_bp</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app = Flask()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.register\_blueprint(admin\_bp)</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page7"></span>**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Use the Flask Blueprint to make routes</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Inside the blueprint you can add routes, like you normally would, just you use</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">the blueprint instance instead of using </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895751168;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895750144"><span style="position:absolute;
left:188px;top:-12px;width:24px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image062.jpg" width="24" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@admin\_bp.route('/', methods=('GET', 'POST'))</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">admin\_index</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Configure and use sessions in Flask</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You must set a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">SECRET\_KEY</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> property in your flask config for sessions to work.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895749120"><span style="position:absolute;left:75px;top:-12px;
width:64px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image063.jpg" width="64" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can import session from flask.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895748096;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask **import** Flask, session</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Then simply use </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> to store things you want to be available later</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895747072;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895746048"><span style="position:absolute;
left:83px;top:-13px;width:47px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image065.jpg" width="47" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">To set something in the session </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'key'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\] = value</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">To get something from the session </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session.get(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'key'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">to remove something from the session </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session.pop(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'key'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use a Jinja template as return for a Flask route with render\_template</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">render\_template</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> method to render the template into a string,</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895745024"><span style="position:absolute;left:41px;top:-13px;
width:92px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image066.jpg" width="92" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">and then return it from your route. You can give it the HTML file and keyword</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">arguments that will be accessible as variables inside the template.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895744000;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@app.route('/')</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">index</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">render\_template(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'index.html'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, sitename=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'My Sample'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Add variables to a Jinja template with {{ }}</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Then inside our HTML we can access the key</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895742976;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;title></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{{ sitename }}</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:navy">&lt;/title></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Check the </span>[<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#4078C0;text-decoration:
none">Jinja2</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333;text-decoration:none"> </span>](https://jinja.palletsprojects.com/en/2.11.x/templates/)<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">docs for all the things you can do in Jinja2 templates.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use include to share template content in Jinja</span>**

**<span style="font-size:14.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;

<span style="position:absolute;

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Connect to a PostgreSQL RDBMS using Psycopg</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895739904;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:162px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image048.jpg" width="967" height="162" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">import </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">psycopg2</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">CONNECTION\_PARAMETERS = {</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'dbname'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'psycopg\_test\_db'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'user'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'psycopg\_test\_user'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'password'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'password'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">with </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">psycopg2.connect(\*\*CONNECTION\_PARAMETERS) **as** conn:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(conn.get\_dsn\_parameters())</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Open a "cursor" to perform data operations</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use the with keyword to clean up connections and database cursors</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895738880;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:162px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image048.jpg" width="967" height="162" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">import </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">psycopg2</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">CONNECTION\_PARAMETERS = {</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'dbname'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'psycopg\_test\_db'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'user'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'psycopg\_test\_user'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'password'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'password'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">with </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">psycopg2.connect(\*\*CONNECTION\_PARAMETERS) **as** conn:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(conn.get\_dsn\_parameters())</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use results performed from executing a SELECT statement on existing database entities</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895737856;left:0px;margin-left:45px;margin-top:37px;width:967px;
height:110px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span><span id="page8"></span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">with </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">psycopg2.connect(\*\*CONNECTION\_PARAMETERS) **as** conn:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">with </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">conn.cursor() **as** curs:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">curs.execute(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'SELECT manu\_year, make, model FROM cars;'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">cars = curs.fetchall()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">car **in** cars:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(car) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># (1993, 'Mazda', 'Rx7')</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use parameterized SQL statements to insert, select, update, and delete data</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895736832;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:201px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image067.jpg" width="967" height="201" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">print\_all\_cars</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">with </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">psycopg2.connect(\*\*CONNECTION\_PARAMETERS) **as** conn:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">with </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">conn.cursor() **as** curs:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">curs.execute(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'SELECT manu\_year, make, model, owner\_id FROM cars;'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">cars = curs.fetchall()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">car **in** cars:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(car)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print\_all\_cars()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Output:</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(1993, 'Mazda', 'Rx7', 1)</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">...additional cars</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:14.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">SQLAlchemy Objectives</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895735808;margin-left:0px;margin-top:9px;width:967px;height:1px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image001.jpg" width="967" height="1" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Describe how to create an "engine" that you will use to connect to a PostgreSQL database instance</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Note: When using Flask-SQLAlchemy you don't have to do this</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895734784;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sqlalchemy **import** create\_engine</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">engine = create\_engine(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"postgresql://sqlalchemy\_test:password@localhost/sqlalchemy\_test"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Describe how the with engine.connect() as connection: block establishes and cleans up a connection to the database</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Note: When using Flask-SQLAlchemy you don't have to do this</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895733760;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:227px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image068.jpg" width="967" height="227" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sqlalchemy **import** create\_engine</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db\_url = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"postgresql://sqlalchemy\_test:password@localhost/sqlalchemy\_test"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">engine = create\_engine(db\_url)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">with </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">engine.connect() **as** connection:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">result = connection.execute(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"""</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">SELECT o.first\_name, o.last\_name, p.name</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">FROM owners o</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">JOIN ponies p ON (o.id = p.owner\_id)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"""</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">row **in** result:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(row\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"first\_name"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\], row\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"last\_name"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\], </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"owns"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, row\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"name"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\])</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">engine.dispose()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Describe how to create a database session from an engine</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Note: When using Flask-SQLAlchemy you don't have to do this</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895732736;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:201px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image067.jpg" width="967" height="201" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sqlalchemy **import** create\_engine</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sqlalchemy.orm **import** sessionmaker</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db\_url = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"postgresql://sqlalchemy\_test:password@localhost/sqlalchemy\_test"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">engine = create\_engine(db\_url)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">SessionFactory = sessionmaker(bind=engine)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session = SessionFactory()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Do stuff with the session</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">engine.dispose()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Create a mapping for SQLAlchemy to use to tie together a class and a table in the database</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Mappings</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Mappings with plain SQLAlchemy</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page9"></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">With just SQLAlchemy we inherit from </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Base</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> and we have to import all the</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895731712"><span style="position:absolute;left:188px;top:-13px;
width:30px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image069.jpg" width="30" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">schema objects and types manually.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895730688;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:227px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image068.jpg" width="967" height="227" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># ponies.py</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sqlalchemy.ext.declarative **import** declarative\_base</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sqlalchemy.schema **import** Column, ForeignKey</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sqlalchemy.types **import** Integer, String</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Base = declarative\_base()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">Pony</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(Base):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_tablename\_\_ = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'ponies'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">id = Column(Integer, primary\_key=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">name = Column(String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">birth\_year = Column(Integer)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">breed = Column(String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner\_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"owners.id"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Mappings with Flask-SQLAlchemy</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">When using Flask-SQLAlchemy we inherit from </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.Model</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> instead of </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Base</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895729664"><span style="position:absolute;left:234px;top:-12px;
width:52px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image070.jpg" width="52" height="15" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895728640"><span style="position:absolute;
left:340px;top:-12px;width:30px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image069.jpg" width="30" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">and we can use all the schema objects and types because Flask-SQLAlchemy</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">attaches them to the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> instance. So we just prefix them with </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895727616"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-12px;
width:967px;height:219px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image071.jpg" width="967" height="219" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># owner.py</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.models **import** db</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">Pony</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(db.Model):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_tablename\_\_ = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'ponies'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary\_key=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">name = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">birth\_year = db.Column(db.Integer)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">breed = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner\_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"owners.id"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Relationships</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">One-to-Many</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Just create the proper foreign key columns on the models, and then</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">define the relationships. *(Remember Flask-SQLAlchemy will need to preface most of these objects with* </span>*<span style="font-size:6.5pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.</span>*<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> *)*</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895726592"><span style="position:absolute;left:505px;top:-11px;
width:24px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image072.jpg" width="24" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Remember the rule of thumb. The "Many" always has the foreign key on it.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895725568;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:357px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image073.jpg" width="967" height="357" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># The one</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">Owner</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(db.Model):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_tablename\_\_ = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"owners"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary\_key=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">first\_name = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">last\_name = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">email = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># ponies belong to an owner</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">ponies = db.relationship(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Pony"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, back\_populates=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">"owner"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># The Many</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">Pony</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(db.Model):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_tablename\_\_ = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"ponies"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary\_key=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">name = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">birth\_year = db.Column(Integer)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">breed = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># The pony contains an owner\_id foreign key</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner\_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">"owners.id"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># An owner has many ponies</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner = db.relationship(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Owner"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, back\_populates=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">"ponies"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Many-to-Many</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Remember that a Many-to-Many relationship is really two One-to-Many relationships</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">with a join table in the middle.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You must create a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Table()</span><span style="font-size:
8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> object and not a model for your join table.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895724544;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895723520"><span style="position:absolute;
left:91px;top:-13px;width:47px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image074.jpg" width="47" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">We define the foreign keys on our join table, which joins the Ponies</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">to thier Handlers.</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony\_handlers = db.Table(</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"pony\_handlers"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.Column(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"pony\_id"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, db.ForeignKey(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">"ponies.id"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), primary\_key=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">),</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.Column(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"handler\_id"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, db.ForeignKey(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">"handlers.id"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), primary\_key=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Then setup the relationships on each Model making sure to define a "secondary"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">keyword argument is set to the table we just made.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895722496;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:149px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image075.jpg" width="967" height="149" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Inside the Pony class...</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">handlers = db.relationship(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Handler"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">secondary=pony\_handlers,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">back\_populates=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"ponies"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Inside the Handler class...</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">ponies = db.relationship(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Pony"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">secondary=pony\_handlers,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">back\_populates=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"handlers"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">On backpopulates</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page10"></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:133%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">If you leave out the backpopulates parameter, then when you create an object and add related data, the opposite relationship won't be populated. For instance assume we have an </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:133%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Owner</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:133%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> instance and we add a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:133%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Pony</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;line-height:133%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> instance to it.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895721472;margin-left:0px;margin-top:13px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895720448"><span style="position:absolute;
left:59px;top:-18px;width:36px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image058.jpg" width="36" height="15" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895719424"><span style="position:absolute;
left:211px;top:-18px;width:30px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image069.jpg" width="30" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner.ponies.append(pony)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">If we do not have </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">backpopulates</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> set to the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> propery of the Pony</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895718400"><span style="position:absolute;left:87px;top:-13px;
width:80px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image076.jpg" width="80" height="15" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895717376"><span style="position:absolute;
left:219px;top:-13px;width:35px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image077.jpg" width="35" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">class, then if you try to look at the owner of the pony like this:</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895716352;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(pony.owner) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Returns None</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Then it will still be None. If you set </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">backpopulates</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> to the owner, then this</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895715328"><span style="position:absolute;left:169px;top:-12px;
width:81px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image039.jpg" width="81" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">will get populates and stay in sync.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">IMPORTANT</span>**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">: backpopulates just controls what happens with the objects *BEFORE*</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">we commit them to the database.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">It's always a good idea to setup your </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">backpopulates</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> properly so you aren't</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895714304"><span style="position:absolute;left:181px;top:-13px;
width:80px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image078.jpg" width="80" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">surprised.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Add data to the database, both single entities as well as related data</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895713280;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:279px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image079.jpg" width="967" height="279" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">you = Owner(first\_name=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"your first name"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">last\_name=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"your last name"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">email=</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"your email"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">your\_pony = Pony(name=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"your pony's name"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">birth\_year=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2020</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">breed=</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"whatever you want"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner=you)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>
