<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Using session with Flask-SQLAlchemy</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">We use this exactly the same as above but we get the session from the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">db</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> instance.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895712256;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895711232"><span style="position:absolute;
left:350px;top:-13px;width:18px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image037.jpg" width="18" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.session.add(you)</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt">           </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Connects you and your\_pony objects</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.session.commit()</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt">           </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Saves data to the database</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">IMPORTANT </span>**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">don't confuse this session with the Flask session. This is a</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">database </span>*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">session while flask session is the *browser* session.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Update data in the database</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895710208;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:188px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image080.jpg" width="967" height="188" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<table class="MsoNormalTable" data-border="0" data-cellspacing="0" data-cellpadding="0" style="margin-left:12.0pt;border-collapse:collapse"><tbody><tr class="odd" style="height:8.85pt"><td width="163" data-valign="bottom" style="width: 122.0pt; padding: 0in 0in 0in 0in; height: 8.85pt"><p><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
  color:#333333">print(your_pony.birth_year)</span></p></td><td width="56" data-valign="bottom" style="width: 42.0pt; padding: 0in 0in 0in 0in; height: 8.85pt"><p><em><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># &gt; 2020</span></em></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Updating is just like setting a property </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">your\_pony.birth\_year = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">2019</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">The pony instance updates immediately</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<table class="MsoNormalTable" data-border="0" data-cellspacing="0" data-cellpadding="0" style="margin-left:12.0pt;border-collapse:collapse"><tbody><tr class="odd" style="height:8.85pt"><td width="163" data-valign="bottom" style="width: 122.0pt; padding: 0in 0in 0in 0in; height: 8.85pt"><p><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Delete data from the database (including cascades!)</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Know how to use and specify the "delete-orphan" cascading strategy</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895709184;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:84px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image045.jpg" width="967" height="84" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Just passing the owner instance to delete, deletes it, but....</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.session.delete(you)</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">It doesn't actually change the database until you commit! </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.session.commit()</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895708160;margin-left:0px;margin-top:29px;width:967px;height:227px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image068.jpg" width="967" height="227" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">Owner</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(db.Model):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_tablename\_\_ = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'owners'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary\_key=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">first\_name = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">last\_name = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">email = db.Column(db.String(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">255</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This is a relationship between Ponies and Owner.</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">We have set it to cascase and delete orphans so</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">when we delete an owner all the ponies related to</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">that owner will be deleted</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">ponies = db.relationship(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Pony"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">back\_populates=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"owner"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">cascade=</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"all, delete-orphan"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Describe the purpose of a Query object</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<table data-cellspacing="0" data-cellpadding="0" data-hspace="0" data-vspace="0" width="68" height="8"><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;" data-valign="top" height="8" style="padding-top: 0in; padding-right: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0in"><p><span id="page11"></span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:79%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">one_or_none</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">When you use SQLAlchemy's querying API, you're not actually immediately executing SQL against the database. Instead, all of the specifications that you add to the query are saved up into a single object that you then use to have SQL executed against the database. This allows you to make decisions at runtime about how you want to apply filters to the query. This will become clearer as you read about how to query and apply filters in the following sections. The important thing to note is that a Query object will not actually do anything with the database unless you explicitly tell it to do something.</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use a Session object to query the database using a model</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">With plain SQLAlchemy</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895707136;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony\_query = session.query(Pony)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(pony\_query)</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895706112;margin-left:0px;margin-top:35px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony\_id\_4\_query = session.query(Pony).get(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">With Flask SQLAlchemy</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Flask SQLAlchemy attaches the </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session.query</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> to the Model directly.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895705088"><span style="position:absolute;left:160px;top:-13px;
width:80px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image081.jpg" width="80" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">So you can re-write any call to </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session.query</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> as </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">&lt;Model>.query</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> .</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895704064;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895703040"><span style="position:absolute;
left:150px;top:-12px;width:179px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image082.jpg" width="179" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This plain SQLAlchemy query: </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony = session.query(Pony).get(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">);</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Can be re-written as:</span>*

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony = Pony.query.get(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">How to order your results</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895702016;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner\_query = Owner.query(Owner.first\_name, Owner.last\_name)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.order\_by(Owner.last\_name)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(owner\_query)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use the filter method to find just what you want</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895700992;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony\_query = Pony.query.filter(Pony.name.like(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"%u%"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony\_query = Pony.query</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.filter(Pony.name.ilike(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"%u%"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.filter(Pony.birth\_year &lt; </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2015</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use instance methods on the Query object to return a list or single item</span>**

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">all </span><span style="font-size:
8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">- returns a list</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895699968"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image083.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895698944"><span style="position:absolute;
left:22px;top:-12px;width:24px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image084.jpg" width="24" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">first </span><span style="font-size:
8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">- returns a single object</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895697920"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-12px;
width:49px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image085.jpg" width="49" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">one </span><span style="font-size:
8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">- returns a single object or raises an exception</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895696896"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;

color:#333333"> - returns a single object or None</span>

<span style="position:absolute;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">ponies = Pony.query.all()</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pony **in** ponies:</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use the count method to … count</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Query objects with criteria on dependant objects</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895691776;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">hirzai\_owners = Owner.query \\</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.join(Pony)</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt">   </span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\\</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.filter(Pony.breed == </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Hirzai"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner **in** hirzai\_owners:</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Lazily load objects</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Eagerly load objects</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895689728;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owners\_and\_ponies = Owner.query.options(joinedload(Owner.ponies))</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;

7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">owner **in** owners\_and\_ponies:</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;

<span id="page12"></span>**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Install the Flask-SQLAlchemy extension to use with Flask</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895688704;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv install Flask psycopg2-binary \\</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">SQLAlchemy Flask-SQLAlchemy</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Configure SQLAlchemy using Flask-SQLAlchemy</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Create a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">SQLALCHEMYDATABASE\_URI</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> property in your Flask app config</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895687680"><span style="position:absolute;left:45px;top:-12px;
width:131px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image087.jpg" width="131" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Then you can pass your app to SQLAlchemy for super simple apps</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895686656;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:149px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image088.jpg" width="967" height="149" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">config **import** Config</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask **import** Flask</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask\_sqlalchemy **import** SQLAlchemy</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app = Flask(\_\_name\_\_)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.config.from\_object(Config)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">We are creating the DB in app.py after creating the app.</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">So we can just pass our app to SQLAlchemy</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db = SQLAlchemy(app)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">However, if you've defined your db object BEFORE your app is created in another module, you must use the </span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">init\_app</span><span style="font-size:
7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> method on db to configure Flask-SQLAlchemy</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895685632;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895684608"><span style="position:absolute;
left:529px;top:-11px;width:52px;height:14px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image089.jpg" width="52" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># models.py</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask\_sqlalchemy **import** SQLAlchemy</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">notice we create the db instance without passing it app </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db = SQLAlchemy()</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">app.py</span>*

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895683584"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-27px;
width:967px;height:175px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image090.jpg" width="967" height="175" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask **import** Flask</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.config **import** Configuration</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">The act of importing this creates the db instance </span>***<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.models **import** db</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">We create our app here</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app = Flask(\_\_name\_\_)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.config.from\_object(Configuration)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">We use init\_app and pass it the app </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.init\_app(app)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Use the convenience functions and objects Flask-SQLAlchemy provides you to use in your code</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Flask-SQLAlchemy adds the query object to every instance of a Model.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895682560;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Pony.query.get(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">It has some Flask specific things such as </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">get\_or\_404</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> , which just throws a</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895681536"><span style="position:absolute;left:202px;top:-12px;
width:64px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image091.jpg" width="64" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">404 error if there's no Pony coming back from the database. There is also a similar </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">first\_or\_404</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> method.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895680512;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895679488"><span style="position:absolute;
left:405px;top:-13px;width:75px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image092.jpg" width="75" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Pony.query.get\_or\_404(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Flask-SQLAlchemy also adds the </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">session</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> object to the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> instance.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895678464;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895677440"><span style="position:absolute;
left:166px;top:-12px;width:46px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image093.jpg" width="46" height="15" /></span></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895676416"><span style="position:absolute;
left:278px;top:-12px;width:19px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image094.jpg" width="19" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.session.add(owner)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.session.commit()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Install Alembic into your project</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run alembic init &lt;directory-name></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Configure Alembic to talk to your database and not have silly migration names</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Add environment variable to </span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">env.py</span>**

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895673344"><span style="position:absolute;left:189px;top:-14px;
width:52px;height:18px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image095.jpg" width="52" height="18" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Import the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">os</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> module</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895672320;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895671296"><span style="position:absolute;
left:53px;top:-13px;width:18px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image096.jpg" width="18" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">import </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">os</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">before </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">run\_migrations\_offline</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> add this line</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895670272;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895669248"><span style="position:absolute;
left:34px;top:-12px;width:131px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image097.jpg" width="131" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">config.set\_main\_option(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"sqlalchemy.url"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, os.environ.get(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">"DATABASE\_URL"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Making better migration file names</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can set this in </span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">alembic.ini</span><span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> so your migration files will have dates in the names.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895668224"><span style="position:absolute;left:92px;top:-11px;
width:69px;height:15px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image098.jpg" width="69" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895667200;margin-left:45px;margin-top:38px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span><span id="page13"></span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">file\_template = </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">%%</span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(year)</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">d</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">%%</span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(month)</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">.2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">d</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">%%</span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(day)</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">.2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">d\_</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">%%</span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(hour)</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">.2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">d</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">%%</span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(minute)</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">.2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">d</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">%%</span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(second)</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">.2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">d\_</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">%%</span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(slug)</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">s</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Control Alembic's ability to migrate your database</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Generating a migration (revision)</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895666176;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run alembic revision -m "create the owners table"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Running a migration (upgrading to a revision)</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895665152;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run alembic upgrade head</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Rolling back a migration (downgrading to a revision)</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895664128;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run alembic downgrade &lt;revision hash></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Rolling back all migrations (downgrading to base)</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895663104;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run alembic downgrade base</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Viewing your migration history (revision history)</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895662080;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run alembic history</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Reason about the way Alembic orders your migrations; and,</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Alembic treats migrations like a linked list. It does not use the dates in the</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">filenames to decide which migrations to run and which order they get run.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Instead each revision has a revision hash, and each revision has a 'down\_revision'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">property that points at the previous revision. (except for the first revision which of course will have it's down\_revision set to None)</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895661056;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image040.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">revision = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'ddbf30c38165'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">down\_revision = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'e363377eb6d7'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Handle branching and merging concerns</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">If two teammates both commit new revisions, then you will end up with a conflict</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">in the down\_revisions. Your revision linked list might look like this:</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895660032;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">--<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">ae1027a6acf (Team A's most recent)</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">/</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">&lt;</span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">-- 1975ea83b712 &lt;--</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\\</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">-- 27c6a30d7c24 (Team B's most recent)</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">and you'll get an error like this:</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895659008;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">FAILED: Multiple </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#0086B3">head</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> revisions are present **for** given argument </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'head'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">;</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">please specify a specific target revision, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">'&lt;branchname>@head'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **to**</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">narrow **to** a specific </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#0086B3">head</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, **or** </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'heads'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **for** all heads</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">you can solve this with a merge specifying the two revisions</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895657984;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run alembic merge -m "merge contracts and devices" ae1027 27c6a</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Configuring a Flask application to use Alembic;</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895656960;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv install alembic Flask-Migrate</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895655936;margin-left:0px;margin-top:34px;width:967px;height:240px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image099.jpg" width="967" height="240" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># app/\_\_init\_\_.py</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.models **import** db</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask **import** Flask</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">config **import** Config</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">We have to import flask\_migrate </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">flask\_migrate **import** Migrate **import** os</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app = Flask(\_\_name\_\_)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Load our config, make sure you set DATABASE\_URL as flask migrate</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">uses it as well</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">app.config.from\_object(Config)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">db.init\_app(app)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">And we have to do this to configure Flask Migrate. It needs to know about</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">both our app and our db object</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Migrate(app, db)</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Run commands to manage your database through the flask command; and,</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page14"></span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">When we use Flask-Migrate we run the commands through the flask command.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Instead of alembic init…</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895654912;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run flask db init</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Check the help for the rest of the commands, which are the same as Alembic</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895653888;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:331px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image100.jpg" width="967" height="331" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run flask db --help</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Usage: flask db \[OPTIONS\] COMMAND \[ARGS\]...</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Perform database migrations.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Options:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">--help  Show this message and exit.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Commands:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">branches</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">current</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">downgrade</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">edit</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">heads</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">history</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">init</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">merge</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">migrate</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">revision</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">show</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">stamp</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">upgrade</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Show current branch points</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Display the current revision for each database.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Revert to a previous version</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Edit a revision file</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Show current available heads in the script directory</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">List changeset scripts in chronological order.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Creates a new migration repository.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Merge two revisions together, creating a new revision file</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Autogenerate a new revision file (Alias for 'revision...</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Create a new revision file.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Show the revision denoted by the given symbol.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">'stamp' the revision table with the given revision; don't run...</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">Upgrade to a later version</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Autogenerate migrations from your models!</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Instead of alembic migrate…</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895652864;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:45px"><img src="week-18-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="967" height="45" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pipenv run flask db migrate -m "create owners table"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">flask db migrate does **magic** now, it reads your models and tries to</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">autogenerate the migration files based on the model.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">IMPORTANT </span>**<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">always check the autogenerated migration though, as there's only</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">so much flask migrate can do and it might not get everything perfectly correct, but it is a time saver!</span>
